 Chhath Puja is one of the major festivals in India
 ye tyohaar bihar, uttar pradesh ke zyaadaatar hisson main or nepal ke bhi kuch bhaagon main manaaya jaataa he
 This Chhath festival lasting four days is dedicated to the Sun God
 is parv main duubate or ugte donon suraj ko arghya diya jaataa he
 On the fourth day, Arghya is offered to the rising sun on the morning of Kartik Shukla Saptami
 parivaar ke achche swasthya or aarthik sthiti main sudhaar kii kaamana se mahilaayein ye vrath karti hai
 During the Chhath festival, Arghya is offered during the sun rising and setting
 iske saath hi ganga main dubkee lagaakar ye tyohaar manaaya jaataa he
 What is the significance of the second arghya in Chhath? On the Chhath festival, the first arghya is given to the setting sun
 is samay jal main doodh daalkar surya kii antim kiran ko arghya diya jaataa he
 With this, by the grace of Lord Shiva and Suryanarayana, the great child of the best child is received
 vahiin iske agle din ugte surat ko arghya diya jaataa he
 There is also a scientific reason behind giving water in the morning
 subah ke samay suryadev ko jal chadhaane se sharir kii rog pratirodhatmak shakti bad jaati he
 Vitamin d from sunlight is completed in the body and skin diseases are less
 bhagwaan surya ke arghydaan kii vishesh mahatta he
 Every morning in the morning, red flowers with rice, blood, rice, etc
, filled with water (copper vessels) filled with water, and chanting Surya Mantra with a happy heart, should offer flowers to Lord Surya by offering Arghya

 An RTI activist was shot dead in Motihari, Bihar
 pichley 6 maah main RTI kaaryakarta kii hatya kaa yah teesraa maamla he
 The deceased were associated with the Civil Rights Forum
 unhone police, prashasan or manaregaa se jude bhrashtachar ke kai maamalon kaa khulaasa kiya tha
 RTI activist Rajendra Singh was returning from Motihari to his village Sangrampur on Tuesday afternoon
 tabhi unako overtek kar ek bike aage nikali
 And then two criminals riding on that bike fired indiscriminately at Rajendra Singh
 is hamale main rajendra singh ko teen goliyaan lagi
 Due to which he died
 jahaan hamalaa kiya gaya, vah bilkul sunsaan jagah thi
 Shivprakash Rai of the Civil Rights Forum said that Rajendra Singh was killed because he was an RTI activist
 raay ke mutabik haal hi main rajendra par jhootha cese karaane ke maamle main court ne sangyaan liya tha
 And action was taken against the then station in-charge of Sangrampur
 isse pehle rajendra singh shikshak niyukti ghotaalaa, manaregaa or indira awaas yojana se jude maamle bhi ujagar kar chuke the
 Shivprakash Rai says that on June 12, when he met Rajendra Singh, he had expressed the possibility of his murder
 isse pehle bhi teen baar un par jaanaleva hamalaa ho chukaa tha
 Meanwhile, Motihari SP Upendra Sharma says that the police is investigating the case
 maamaal pariwarik ranjish kaa bhi lagata he kyonki unki patni ne police ko di gai shikaayat main sampatti vivaad kaa bhi ullekh kiya he
 The police is investigating the matter from every angle
 bataa den ki bihar main is saal artiai kaaryakarta kihatyaka yah teesraa maamla he
 Earlier, one RTI worker has been murdered in Vaishali and Saharsa

 World Sleep Day 2019: World Sleep Day is celebrated on 15 March every year worldwide

 The purpose of celebrating World Sleep Day is to make people aware of the benefits to health from sleeping 7-8 hours
 kai study main is baat kii pushti ho chuki he ki neend kii kami ke kaaran logon ko dil kii beemaari, stroke, hai blad pressure, diabetes ke saath vajan badhane kii samasya bhi ho sakati he
 Yes, good and adequate amount of sleep, diet and exercise is just as important to lose weight
 kam sone ke saath anheldi lifestil, diet, tanaav bhi vajan badhane ke liye jimmedaar hote hai
 According to the Health Expert, lack of sleep affects the body's ghrelin and leptin hormones
 sharir main ghrelin hormone ke nikalne par bhukh kaa zyada ehsaas hota he
 This hormone weakens metabolism and deposits fat in the body
 vahiin, leptin hormone sharir kii fat koshikaon se nikalataa he
 These hormones reduce appetite
 sharir main leptin hormone ke kam maatra main banane se bhukh zyada lagati he, jis kaaran aap jarurat se zyada kha lete hai
 It works to increase your weight
 bataa den, neend puri naa hone se sharir main leptin hormone kaa str kam hota he or ghrelin hormone kaa str badhata he

 niyantran rekha ke paar hamale kootnithik safalataa adhik thi

 tippaniyan The book, published from Penguin Random House, states, "if it has international support for attacks across the Line of Control, it is because the jihadist attack from Pakistan has been controlled by India very carefully since 1998

 The Central Board of Secondary Education has started the board exams of Class 10 from today
 is pariksha main kareeb 18
 5 lakh candidates will participate
 is baar niyamit chaatro ke liye khaas niyam hai or ummidavaar pariksha ke vakt in baton kaa dhyaan rakhen
 If you too are going to participate in this exam, then you have to keep these things in mind
 
 
 uniform kaa rakhen dhyaan-is baar niyamit chaatro ke liye skool uniform anivaary kar di gai he
 According to the new rules of the board, regular students are required to wear their school uniform
 sirf privet chaatr hi cajual kapadon main aa sakate hai
 If students do not come in uniform, they can be stopped for entry in the examination center
 10 baje ke baad nahin milegi entry:pariksha centre main koi bhi chaatr subah 10 baje entry letaa he to unhen entry nahin di jaaegi
 Therefore all students and their parents are advised to ensure that they arrive at the centers on time and take care of time
 admit card kaa dhyaan rakhen-admit card aisa dastavej he jo aapako pariksha centre par le janaa aavashyak he or iske bina chaatro ko skool main pravesh nahin diya jayega
 Also check whether the school's seal and necessary signature have been done on it
 biimaar chaatr ke liye khaas vyavastha-jo chaatr biimaar hai yaa unhen koi dikkat he to apane saath khaane kaa saamaan bhi le ja sakate hai
 Diabetes patients can also take food items with them
 time management-paper ko jaldi karne kaa sabase sahi tarika he time management
 Whenever you sit for paper, then those sections which are of higher number, first solve them
 phir kam number vaala section hal kerani ke koshish kerani chahie
 Or tackle those questions for which you are absolutely confident
